	<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of public art in Philadelphia</h1>
	
	<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
		<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="noprint infobox" id="GeoGroup" style="width: 23em; font-size: 88%; line-height: 1.5em">

<tbody><tr>
<td><b>Map all coordinates using:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/osm4wiki/cgi-bin/wiki/wiki-osm.pl?project=en&amp;article=List_of_public_art_in_Philadelphia">OpenStreetMap</a> 
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><b>Download coordinates as:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/kmlexport?article=List_of_public_art_in_Philadelphia">KML</a> <b>·</b> <a class="external text" href="http://tripgang.com/kml2gpx/http%3A%2F%2Ftools.wmflabs.org%2Fkmlexport%3Farticle%3DList_of_public_art_in_Philadelphia?gpx=1" rel="nofollow">GPX</a>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable plainlinks" role="note">This list is <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Lists#Incomplete_lists" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Lists">incomplete</a>; you can help by <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_public_art_in_Philadelphia&amp;action=edit">expanding it</a>.</div>
<p>This is a <b>list of <a href="/wiki/Public_art" title="Public art">public artworks</a> in <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a></b>.  The <a href="/wiki/Association_for_Public_Art" title="Association for Public Art">Association for Public Art</a> estimates the city has thousands of public artworks;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> the Smithsonian lists more than 700.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>  Since 1959 nearly 400 works of public art have been created as part of the city's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Percent_for_Art" title="Percent for Art">Percent for Art</a> program, the first such program in the U.S.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p><p>This list contains only works of public art in outdoor public spaces, and not, for example, works inside museums.  Most of the works mentioned are sculptures. Other kinds of art, i.e., <a href="/wiki/Sound_installation" title="Sound installation">sound installations</a>, are marked as such next to their titles.
</p>
